Comment Key: LabTestRecommendation
Comment Value: 1. Increased Eosinophils on white cell count. This is linked to your allergies and skin problems. It will revert when these inflammatory conditions improve.
2. Raised uric acid. Drink enough water and less very sweet fruit. Monitor and if any joint pains review this with your doctor.
3. Raised total and LDL cholesterol. Increase cardiovascular exercise raising heart rate 3-5x a week. Review with your doctor in 3-6 months. If not improving consider medication for familial cholesterol.
Triglycerides and liver enzymes normal (considering previous Roaccutane)
4. Raised ultra sensitive CRP indicate moderate levels of background inflammation. This is most likely affected by your skin and allergies. Review once your skin has improved.

There are no major red flags that need to be addressed immediately, rather refine your everyday lifestyle choices for improved future health. These adjustments take a good 3-6 months to show change. Repeat the tests that were abnormal after this time frame to review. It was a pleasure giving you feedback for your comprehensive medical! Dr Janine
Comment Key: LabTestRecommendation
Comment Value: 1. Increased Eosinophils on white cell count. This is linked to your allergies and skin problems. It will revert when these inflammatory conditions improve.
2. Raised uric acid. Drink enough water and less very sweet fruit. Monitor and if any joint pains review this with your doctor.
3. Raised total and LDL cholesterol. Increase cardiovascular exercise raising heart rate 3-5x a week. Review with your doctor in 3-6 months. If not improving consider medication for familial cholesterol.
Triglycerides and liver enzymes normal (considering previous Roaccutane)
4. Raised ultra sensitive CRP indicate moderate levels of background inflammation. This is most likely affected by your skin and allergies. Review once your skin has improved.
